                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-101180351002">
                      The Max Amount of Weight You Could Realistically Gain in One Day
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-101180351002" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">

                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <span class="author-name Font-C-2-140 D-b">
                            <a class="attribution-name Font-C-2-140 Fw-b Whs-n" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:83d8f107-2016-3c10-8509-52f119034bd0;t9:17;elm:itm;elmt:link;itc:0" href="http://www.womenshealthmag.com/" style="color:#000;" target="_blank">
                             Women's Health
                            </a>
                           </span>
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             October 28, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-101180351002" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <img alt="The Max Amount of Weight You Could Realistically Gain in One Day" height="333" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/e9bccb1f29bcb5732d776aab8b3d647cf00a7499.jpg" width="500"/>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Everyone fears the consequence of a diet that has gone off the rails.
                           </strong>
                           (Food Collection/Offset)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           By Annie Daly for Womens Health
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Of course you try your very best to stick to a relatively healthy diet and exercise plan. But some days, youre bound to go overboardafter all, youre only human. Perhaps its that time of the month and you just cant stop munching; perhaps you had one too many margs at happy hour and find yourself housing enough tacos at dinner to win an eating contest; or perhaps youre so overtired that you double up on breakfast because your stomach feels like a bottomless pit. Point is, everyone overindulges on occasion. But while its easy to freak out and think you blew your diet, dontbecause you didnt.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          We asked Samantha Cassetty, R.D., M.S., nutrition director at Luvo, just how much weight you can realistically gain in one terrible, horrible, no good, very bad (eating) day. And it turns out, youd have to take in a
                          <em>
                           ridiculous
                          </em>
                          amount of food to gain even just a pound in one day.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Its virtually impossible to gain weight overnight, even if you really blew it on bar food, says Cassetty. The reason comes down to calorie math. Though its not 100 percent precise, the basic principle stands true: In order to gain weight, youd have to eat 3,500
                          <em>
                           more
                          </em>
                          calories than you typically eat and burn off to maintain your figure. So lets say you eat 2,000 calories per day on a normal day. Youd have to eat 3,500
                          <em>
                           additional
                          </em>
                          calories, totaling 5,500 calories, to gain a single pound. And thats not even taking any physical activity into account.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          What does 3,500 calories look like, exactly? To get 3,500 more calories, you could eat your regular diet and then also have three glasses of wine (370 calories), two chicken wings (110 calories), some onion rings (340 calories), a portion of chips and queso (290 calories), one burger with the works (860 calories), and a slice of chocolate cake (795 calories). Thats a lot of foodand you havent even hit the mark yet! says Cassetty.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Theres even more scientific evidence that its pretty hard to gain real weight after one day of overeating: Although people typically say they gain five to 10 pounds over the six-week holiday period, the best study to date, published in the
                          <em>
                           New England Journal of Medicine
                          </em>
                          , found that, on average, most people gained just one, says Cassetty. Fewer than 10 percent of the study participants actually gained more than five pounds between Thanksgiving and New Years Day.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Of course, a bad diet day could leave you feeling incredibly bloated and just ugh the next day. But as long as you course correct the next dayi.e., you
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:83d8f107-2016-3c10-8509-52f119034bd0;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.womenshealthmag.com/weight-loss/what-to-do-after-eating-too-much?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_StopOvereating" target="_blank">
                           eat responsibly
                          </a>
                          and get back to your
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:83d8f107-2016-3c10-8509-52f119034bd0;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.womenshealthmag.com/fitness?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_FitnessChannel" target="_blank">
                           fitness routine
                          </a>
                          youll keep the real pounds from piling on, says Cassetty. So as you go into the holiday season, remember: Its okay if you love your moms cooking so much that you eat a lot of it. Just dont make a habit of it, and be sure to stay consistent with your gym routine.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          And if you
                          <em>
                           do
                          </em>
                          get off track in a more significant way,
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:83d8f107-2016-3c10-8509-52f119034bd0;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.womenshealthmag.com/weight-loss/post-weight-gain-tips?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_NotToDoAfterWeightGain" target="_blank">
                           check out what
                           <em>
                            not
                           </em>
                           to do after youve gained weight
                          </a>
                          .
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                           </strong>
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:83d8f107-2016-3c10-8509-52f119034bd0;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.womenshealthmag.com/weight-loss/healthy-bedtime-snacks?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_BedtimeSnacksWeightLoss" target="_blank">
                            The 8 Best Bedtime Snacks for Weight Loss
                           </a>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                        </div>

                      <div class="item-text">
                       <div class="item-tag Tt-u Font-C-1-115 Fw-b" style="margin-left:175px;">
                        <a class="tag" data-action-outcome="navigate" data-ylk="g:78fec784-fa89-3a4b-afe9-5fbd6ca58e0f;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:also;ad:0;cpos:3;itc:0;t9:48;elm:itm;elmt:cat" href="/health/tagged/mind" style="color:#999;">
                         Mind
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <a data-action-outcome="open" data-routable-url="/health/1/when-to-take-sleeping-pills-123583633168.html" data-ylk="g:78fec784-fa89-3a4b-afe9-5fbd6ca58e0f;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:also;ad:0;cpos:3;itc:0;t8:tileview;t9:21;elm:img;elmt:ct;" href="/health/when-to-take-sleeping-pills-123583633168.html" style="color:#000;">
                        <span class="item-title Font-A-3-120 D-b" style="word-wrap:break-word;margin-left:175px;">
                         When to Take Sleeping Pills

Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you&#x2019;ve ever wondered about how safe popping a few sleeping pills can actually be, you&#x2019;re not alone: In the last few years, researchers have linked the drugs to higher instances of early death, Alzheimer&#x2019;s, increased mortality, and most recently, a doubled risk of car crashes. Such facts make it tough to tell whether you should risk your health for a decent night&#x2019;s sleep. According to sleep specialists and neurologists, there&#x2019;s a smart way to use sleep remedies, whether they&#x2019;re the over-the-counter variety, or prescribed by your doctor. And while natural remedies will usually&#xA0;trump chemical concoctions, you can safely use these drugs as long as you follow a few guidelines, know your body, and understand their biggest risks.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F9-ways-lack-of-sleep-is-killing-you-20140416?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E 9 Ways Lack of Sleep Is Killing You\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EOnly when you absolutely have to.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"790\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fe6ec3b9f7ab1b6a93c4ee1f2fe544fb2b9668e1e.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe safest and healthiest way to use sleeping pills is &#x201C;to avoid them as much as possible unless absolutely needed,&#x201D; says Dr. Mark Boulos, a neurologist at Toronto&#x2019;s Sunnybrook Health Science, citing &#x201C;the night before you go in for surgery, or for only a few days at a time during stressful times in life&#x201D; as good examples. Columbia neurology professor Dr. Carl Bazil adds that before going in for any pill treatment either at the pharmacy or with your doctor, first take a look at your sleeping habits since these could be the roots of your problem. &#x201C;People don&#x2019;t often think about it, but stimulants late in the day like caffeine, chocolate, or nicotine keep people awake,&#x201D; he says. Then there&#x2019;s your smartphone or tablet, whose light tends to trick your body into thinking it isn&#x2019;t bedtime yet. &#x201C;If you&#x2019;re working up to the time you go to bed, you won&#x2019;t be able to just turn it off,&#x201D; Bazil says. &#x201C;You need time to lie down and let your brain relax.&#x201D; If you&#x2019;ve checked your habits and you&#x2019;re still having trouble sleeping, that&#x2019;s when you should consider a pill.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E1\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F10-common-bad-habits-and-how-to-break-them-20150108?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E0 Common Bad Habits and How to Break Them\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EAfter reading the ingredients.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"405\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F96e3d8119329dcc0ac1c21362cc742652b03dbf3.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBoth over-the-counter and prescription pills can be dangerous if used in high doses, so it&#x2019;s all about using the drugs properly, says Boulos. Bazil adds you can start with over the counter medicines, but know what&#x2019;s in your pills, first. The most popular pharmacy-available medicines contain antihistamine &#x2014; the main ingredient that makes you drowsy. &#x201C;The main problem with antihistamines in many OTC sleep remedies is they last too long,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;So you still have to be aware that you could still be drowsy the next day from the medicine, not from lack of sleep.&#x201D; Other OTC drugs have melatonin, a hormone, which helps re-train and set your body clock if you&#x2019;re trying to regulate your sleeping time. You can also opt for herbal remedies, like Valerian, or supplements with amino acids. But keep in mind there are several signs you should see a doctor, Bazil says. If your sleep troubles are persistent, you get enough sleep but still feel sleepy, or if you wake up frequently, or with headaches, you could have a disorder.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EYou have enough time for them.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"415\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F65f722715ea83f5f4fea341dd88700be6ca950fc.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESleeping pills, by definition, mess with your body&#x2019;s natural behavior (their biggest effects include sedation, slurred speech, and uncoordinated actions) so be extra cautious of when you take them &#x2014;&#xA0;and make no plans to do anything important but sleep for that block of time. &#x201C;Remember these [pills] are meant to make you drowsy, and some of them have the tendency to make you forget things,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;That&#x2019;s all fine if you go to sleep, but some people won&#x2019;t feel sleepy, so they&#x2019;ll decide to take it, and wait until they do feel drowsy.&#x201D; The problem is, the sedative&#x2019;s effects can hit you quickly at unexpected times, like while driving. &#x201C;All of a sudden you&#x2019;re half asleep, which can result in confused or dangerous behavior,&#x201D; Bazil says. A&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Farchpsyc.jamanetwork.com\u002Farticle.aspx?articleid=1885708\"\u003E2014 CDC report\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;found that a high number of emergency room visits were caused by adverse reactions to Ambien, the most popular prescription insomnia-aid &#x2013; and they included a high number of falls, confused behavior, and difficulty waking up. The&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fda.gov\u002FDrugs\u002FDrugSafety\u002Fucm334041.htm\"\u003EFDA also warns\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;about &#x201C;next-morning impairment&#x201D;, or when the drug&#x2019;s effects last longer than you&#x2019;d think. Bazil says since sleeping pills are long acting, even when you wake up, there&#x2019;s a possibility that you&#x2019;re still in a confused state and not 100 percent alert. The lesson is simple: Always follow the recommended dose, and take sleeping pills right before you hit the sack, allowing extra time for any lingering after-effects.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F10-products-to-help-you-get-a-better-nights-sleep-20140310?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E10 Products to Help You Get a Better Night&#x2019;s Sleep\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EIf you&#x2019;re not already hooked.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"361\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fe112e22e08987ddbc01c5aba53715ebbae0bdfd2.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENot all sleeping pills are made equal (Ambien is thought to be less addictive in its ingredients than benzodiazepines like Xanax) but treat all with caution: Whatever you&#x2019;re taking, your body still adapts and becomes immune to sleeping pills fast &#x2014;&#xA0;neutralizing their effect and often tricking you into thinking you need a higher dosage. &#x201C;With on-going use, [the drug&#x2019;s] effectiveness wears off,&#x201D; Boulos says. &#x201C;At this point, the user needs to increase the dose and then it turns into a vicious cycle &#x2014;&#xA0;increased dose, effect of medication wears off, increased dose again and so on.&#x201D; You&#x2019;ll know when you&#x2019;ve used sleeping pills too much when their effectiveness starts to wear off, Boulos says, so avoid daily or regular use so you don&#x2019;t reach that point.\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F8-most-addictive-legal-drugs-20140226?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E \u003Ci\u003E8 Most Addictive Legal Drugs\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EWhen you&#x2019;re sober and off other medications\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F4ca85a31d985090db73a707f2b54344ac275cac6.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;The biggest danger associated with sleeping pills is if they are overdosed or mixed with alcohol or another sedating medication,&#x201D; says Boulos. &#x201C;This can be deadly, as has been the case with several celebrities over the past few years.&#x201D; That&#x2019;s because alcohol, a depressant, intensifies the sedative, drowsy effect of sleeping pills &#x2014;&#xA0;putting you at a bigger risk for injuries resulting from confused behavior. Read the label on your medicine: Don&#x2019;t drink within 24 hours of taking a pill and check with your pharmacist or doctor about any current medications you&#x2019;re taking before starting a new treatment.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EAfter fully assessing your sleep habits.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"764\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F62b60a2f4e3da45a40592b3e3d04eed1e9c8dec3.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe sleeping pill shouldn&#x2019;t be your cop-out for bad sleep behavior. According to Bazil, it&#x2019;s easy to believe that if you take a sleeping pill, you can still have terrible sleeping habits, including working up until the last minute at night or leaving your phone on. &#x201C;They&#x2019;ll expect the pill to overcome all those problems, or make up for not sleeping enough,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;It won&#x2019;t. You still need to pay attention to your body to prepare yourself for sleep, and give adequate time for it.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002Fsigns-you-might-have-a-sleep-disorder-20150504?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003ESigns You Might Have a Sleep Disorder\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThe natural remedies don&#x2019;t work.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fb91a7c91ad61ebf50401de4af598d15c7e2e7901.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E9Photo Courtesy of Getty Images0\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA whole host of new studies show that natural alternatives like&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fhealth-fitness\u002Fhealth\u002Fhow-meditation-can-help-you-sleep-better-20150225\"\u003Emindfulness meditation\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;and even&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fhealth-fitness\u002Fhealth\u002Fa-diet-to-help-get-your-sleep-back-on-track-20140718\"\u003Echanging your dinner diet\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;can help you get to sleep easier. In a recent&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fannals.org\u002Farticle.aspx?articleid=2301405\"\u003Emeta-analysis of 20 studies\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, researchers found that cognitive behavioral therapy worked very similar to&#xA0;medicine for people with insomnia, but without the sedated side effects. You could also make some personal time to de-stress: Boulos recommends doing a relaxing activity before bedtime, like a massage with your significant other, or having a warm shower.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy Jillian Rose Lim \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore From Men&#x2019;s Things That Make You Lose Your Voice","summary":"I havent had a cold in months, but I keep losing my voice.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fd92819b26b5fdcce558afbf8268ac4431d447a7c.jpg\" alt=\"4 Things That Make You Lose Your Voice\" width=\"540\" height=\"279\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EI haven&#x2019;t had a cold in months, but I keep losing my voice. What&#x2019;s going on? \u003C\u002Fb\u003E(\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ELaryngitis (the most common cause of hoarseness or voice loss) happens when your voice box becomes irritated or inflamed, leading to swelling that keeps your vocal cords from being able to open and close smoothly. (This vocal cord movement is what creates sound.) A viral infection, like a cold or the flu, is the usual culprit, but it&#x2019;s not the only one.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EStrain is also a top cause of laryngitis; just one night of cheering at a sporting event or concert can bring it on. Voice strain should go away on its own with rest and lots of fluids. But you really have to rest your voice, especially if you&#x2019;ve lost it entirely: Not only will staying quiet help you heal faster, but taxing your voice during laryngitis can damage vocal cords further and can lead to the formation of polyps or nodules that may require surgery.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.health.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fgallery\u002F0,,20640098,00.html?xid=yahoo-voice-070615\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E10 Ways to Soothe a Sore Throat\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf hoarseness persists beyond a few weeks or keeps coming back, there may be something else going on. One possibility is acid reflux. When stomach acid comes back up the esophagus, it can cause irritation of the vocal cords. The type of reflux most associated with voice issues is called laryngopharyngeal reflux disease, and it often doesn&#x2019;t cause heartburn or nausea. Your doctor can prescribe antacids and other medication (like steroids) that can help your voice if it&#x2019;s not getting better.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnother possible cause is a yeast infection in your throat, also called oral thrush. This appears most often in people with depressed immune systems, like those with HIV or cancer, but people using a corticosteroid inhaler to treat their asthma are also more prone. That&#x2019;s because the steroid can locally decrease your immune function, which allows the overgrowth of yeast. Oral antifungals can solve it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.health.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fgallery\u002F0,,20529772,00.html?xid=yahoo-voice-070615\"\u003E11 Surprising Symptoms of Acid Reflux\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETo get a diagnosis, see an ear, nose and throat specialist (ENT), who can take a look at your vocal cords with a scope to determine if acid reflux or yeast is robbing you of your voice. An ENT can also rule out something more serious, like laryngeal cancer, which often occurs with ear pain and a sore throat on top of voice issues.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EHealth&#x2018;s medical editor, Roshini Rajapaksa, MD, is assistant professor of medicine at the NYU School of Medicine and co-founder of Tula Skincare.\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore from Health.com:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca I Don&#x2019;t Think I&#x2019;d Do It Again.\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhen it comes to pet health costs, is it worth it?&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E(Photo: Makovsvet\u002FGetty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EEven as I said it, I knew it was ridiculous and selfish. &#x201C;Just promise you&#x2019;ll make it till my 30th birthday,&#x201D; I said quietly to Kitty, my tiny ten-year-old cat. We were both underneath my bed, where she&#x2019;d decamped the minute we returned home from a long day at the vet. Earlier that day, she&#x2019;d been diagnosed with a terminal heart condition. Nearly two and a half years later, she&#x2019;d die from it, in a cold and unfamiliar emergency room in the middle of the night.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F01\u002Fokay-to-be-an-overbearing-pet-parent.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E It&#x2019;s Okay to Be an Overbearing Pet Parent\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThis was a longer prognosis than any vet predicted, and yet, in the months since her death, I can&#x2019;t stop wondering whether I did the right thing in delaying the inevitable for so long. The twice-a-day pills, the bimonthly visits to the veterinary cardiologist (which almost always included a chest tap, a risky, invasive procedure that drained fluid from in and around her lungs), not to mention the vast sums of money spent on it all: Were these things really for her, or were they mostly, selfishly, for me? Saying good-bye to a pet has never been easy, but advances in modern veterinary care can make it near-impossible for pet owners to know when to let go. It&#x2019;s an ethical quandary that&#x2019;s in some ways unsettlingly similar \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F10\u002Fatul-gawande-on-being-mortal.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003Eto aging and end-of-life issues currently plaguing human medicine\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Just because we can extend a life, should we?\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOnce, the biggest moral dilemma veterinarians faced was that pet owners were hasty and thoughtless in their decision to euthanize, requesting the procedure at the first sign of age, illness, or mere inconvenience. Now it&#x2019;s often the opposite extreme, said Bernard Rollin, a professor of philosophy and animal sciences at Colorado State University, who in 2011 wrote a\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\u002Fpubmed\u002F21601753\"\u003E paper\u003C\u002Fa\u003E for the journal \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.elsevier.com\u002Fjournals\u002Fveterinary-clinics-of-north-america-small-animal-practice\u002F0195-5616\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Ca\u003EVeterinary Clinics of North America\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Small Practice about the stress this causes veterinarians. &#x201C;In a major ironic twist of fate, rather than human medicine learning the wisdom of euthanasia for suffering animals from veterinary medicine &#x2026; veterinary medicine assimilated some of the more pernicious aspects of human medicine,&#x201D; Rollin wrote. &#x201C;In particular, as animals became increasingly viewed as members of the family, the reluctance to euthanize began to enter veterinary medicine.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA pet is not a person, and the end-of-life decisions for each are not the same. As science writer Carl Safina explains the distinction in his forthcoming\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.amazon.com\u002FBeyond-Words-What-Animals-Think\u002Fdp\u002F0805098887\"\u003E book\u003C\u002Fa\u003E Beyond Words: What Animals Think and Feel, &#x201C;I don&#x2019;t mean to imply that I value the life of a fish or a bird the same way I value a human life, but their presence in the world has as much validity as does our presence.&#x201D; It&#x2019;s not the same, but each life still has value in its own way.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F01\u002Fhow-pets-help-kids-with-autism.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EHow Pets Help Kids With Autism\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnd Rollin is right about the pets-as-family idea. A 2013\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.avma.org\u002FKB\u002FResources\u002FStatistics\u002FPages\u002FMarket-research-statistics-US-Pet-Ownership-Demographics-Sourcebook.aspx\"\u003E survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E by the American Veterinary Medical Association found that two thirds of dog owners consider the animal part of their family, up from just over half in a 2006 survey. (The numbers are lower for cats, but they also show an upward trend.) &#x201C;The human-animal bond has grown &#x2014; it&#x2019;s accepted, it&#x2019;s recognized, I think, at least in part because of the change of social structure in families,&#x201D; said Jane Shaw, a professor of veterinary medicine at Colorado State University. She&#x2019;s referring to the rise in \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nbcnews.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fhealth-news\u002Fnew-normal-cohabitation-rise-study-finds-f1C9208429\"\u003Ecohabitation\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.pewsocialtrends.org\u002F2010\u002F06\u002F25\u002Fchildlessness-up-among-all-women-down-among-women-with-advanced-degrees\u002F\"\u003Echildlessness\u003C\u002Fa\u003E among Americans, or of the increased number of those who are putting \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftwentysomethingmarriage.org\u002F\"\u003Emarriage off\u003C\u002Fa\u003E or never \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.pewsocialtrends.org\u002F2014\u002F09\u002F24\u002Frecord-share-of-americans-have-never-married\u002F\"\u003Egetting around to it at all\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. There are more ways to form families these days, and, as a result, &#x201C;pets are filling a big role for many people,&#x201D; Shaw said. &#x201C;And it means many people are willing to invest the same level of care for their animals as they are for human families.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAmericans spent $56 billion on their pets in 2013, according to the latest figures from the Federal Trade Commission; of that, $7.6 billion went to prescription and over-the-counter drugs for cats and dogs. That&#x2019;s\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.ftc.gov\u002Fsystem\u002Ffiles\u002Fdocuments\u002Freports\u002Fcompetition-pet-medications-industry-prescription-portability-distribution-practices\u002F150526-pet-meds-report.pdf\"\u003E expected\u003C\u002Fa\u003E to grow to $10.2 billion annually by 2018. Indeed, many pet owners are willing to shell out substantial amounts of money on veterinary care: In a 2010\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fsurveys.ap.org\u002Fdata%5CGfK%5CAP-GfK%20Petside%20Topline%20for%20final%20060710_4th%20release.pdf\"\u003E survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of more than a thousand pet owners, 42 percent said they&#x2019;d be somewhat to very likely to spend $5,000 on a single treatment for their pets. Tara Parker-Pope of the New York Times\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwell.blogs.nytimes.com\u002F2010\u002F06\u002F09\u002Fhow-much-would-you-spend-on-a-sick-pet\u002F?_r=0\"\u003E noted\u003C\u002Fa\u003E that the pet owner&#x2019;s annual income did not make a difference in their answers &#x2014; those earning $50,000 per year answered similarly to those earning more.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut the cost of treatment for a slow-acting illness like Kitty&#x2019;s was deceptively exorbitant. I could never agree to pay $5,000 in one go, but $300 here, $75 there? The smaller costs added up. By the end, I was spending about $150 per month on medication and $300 to $800 every other month on visits to a specialist; once, I paid more than $2,000 for an overnight stay in a\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.veterinaryspecialtycare.com\u002Fsurgical-careChamber.php?1\"\u003E hyperbaric oxygen chamber\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, to help her breathing return to normal. I felt equal parts panicky over the expenses and guilty over my mounting financial anxiety, and I noticed that when discussing treatment, the question never seemed to be what was best in the long run for Kitty (or for me, for that matter).\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F07\u002Fdogs-can-get-jealous-suggests-adorable-study.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EDogs Can Get Jealous, Suggests Adorable Study\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENot so long ago, even if you&#x2019;d wanted to drop thousands on a pet&#x2019;s medical care, it wasn&#x2019;t an option. Eleven years ago, Cornell \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.vet.cornell.edu\u002Fnews\u002Farticles\u002Fmri.htm\"\u003Edeveloped\u003C\u002Fa\u003E the first MRI machine designed for pets. Six years ago, some vets began \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.usatoday.com\u002Fstory\u002Fnews\u002Fnation\u002F2014\u002F02\u002F05\u002Fpets-stem-cell-treatment\u002F5224363\u002F\"\u003Eoffering \u003C\u002Fa\u003Estem-cell therapy for dogs, to ease the symptoms of chronic illnesses like arthritis. In many respects, advances like these are a wonderful thing, both for the animals and the people who love them. Initially for Kitty, a chest tap would buy her several solid months of easier breathing, so her vets and I decided the temporary discomfort of the 20-or-so-minute procedure was worth the cost (financial for me, psychic for &#x2014; well, for both of us). They warned me that a time would come when she&#x2019;d need them much more frequently, and the risk and distress would outweigh the benefits. But for the moment, they assured, things were okay. I focused on the moment.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf I&#x2019;m ever in this situation again, though, I&#x2019;ll look farther ahead. As it stands now, Americans have the chance to ensure that their pets get the planned, peaceful exits out of this world that their human loved ones \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fdaily\u002Fintelligencer\u002F2014\u002F11\u002Fdeath-with-dignity-backer-brittany-maynard-dies.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003Eoften do not\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. &#x201C;In the end, you have to make a judgment, one that we&#x2019;re socially not in a position where we make it for ourselves or for our relatives,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;But you are forced to make it for the animal. I like to think of death as a closing to a life. &#x2026; And you don&#x2019;t want the animal to close on its life in misery.&#x201D; In hindsight, I can see the point I should&#x2019;ve shifted course to planning a good death for Kitty rather than stubbornly fighting for her life. Last summer, the chest taps started increasing in frequency &#x2014; once, she needed three in a month. &#x201C;These are not benign and have the potential to cause bleeding,&#x201D; the emergency vet wrote in the medical records after the third one, adding that each tap created inflammation and scar tissue. And yet her vets and I decided to stay the course; even as the taps increased to every other month, the cardiologist (whom I liked very much) and I never spoke of prepping for the end of her life.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut then, even veterinarians struggle with these decisions. Rollin believes he hung on too long to a German shepherd he once had; the dog developed a degenerative spinal disease, and after a while, it couldn&#x2019;t walk. &#x201C;I&#x2019;d come home six, seven times a day and move him, so he didn&#x2019;t get bedsores,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;I think now: Was that the right thing to do? I think, now, that I waited too long.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fthecut\u002F2014\u002F12\u002Fcelebrity-pets-with-big-personalities.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E33 Celebrity Pets With Big Personalities\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt&#x2019;s so hard to know, in part because veterinary end-of-life care comes with complications that don&#x2019;t apply to human medicine. For one, with animals, there is the tiny matter that the patient can&#x2019;t speak. For another, pets can&#x2019;t comprehend the trade-off they&#x2019;re making in enduring the pain and terror of medical treatment now for the promise of more time later. &#x201C;All they know is, This hurts now,&#x201D; Rollin told me. &#x201C;And they look up at you, and they want you to make it stop. And if you&#x2019;re doing it for eight months to garner another three months &#x2014; you see what I mean? I don&#x2019;t think that&#x2019;s fair to the animal. The animal doesn&#x2019;t know anything about the last three months. It&#x2019;s just miserable. And thank God, really, we&#x2019;re in a position to give them a decent death.&#x201D; For some pet owners, a decent death means turning\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fpetrequiem.com\u002Fabout-us\u002F\"\u003E to pet hospice\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, or in-home euthanasia; for others, it&#x2019;s a conversation with their regular vet about making the decision to euthanize before an emergency situation forces it. In either case, it takes an enormous amount of unselfish courage to recognize when it&#x2019;s best for the animal to let them go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIn Atul Gawande&#x2019;s 2014 book\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F10\u002Fatul-gawande-on-being-mortal.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E Being Mortal\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, he talks about how to make the final years of life meaningful for the aged and the ill. Before your loved one gets truly incapacitated in sickness, Gawande suggests clarifying what, exactly, makes life worth living for them. One man&#x2019;s list, memorably recounted in the book, was very short: ice cream and college football. As long as he&#x2019;s well and alert enough to eat his favorite food and watch his favorite football team, he&#x2019;s happy. Again: Pets are not people. But the lesson here applies. &#x201C;When the animal gets very sick, particularly with a terminal disease like cancer,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;you consult that list, and you make sure your own needs, your own guilt, are not prolonging the animal&#x2019;s suffering.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI know what Kitty&#x2019;s would have included: Watching East 73rd Street from the bedroom window, something she did with such intense focus my boyfriend Andrew and I called it Cat TV. Jumping on top of one of us when we went to bed, to sleep perched on one of our backs or sides. Wolfing down the can of Fancy Feast before I barely had the chance to dump it in her bowl. I said earlier that pets can&#x2019;t speak, but, then &#x2014; that&#x2019;s not entirely true, is it? They can&#x2019;t literally talk, but\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F04\u002Fyour-cat-is-trying-to-talk-to-you.html\"\u003E they can and do communicate\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. And when they stop doing the things they&#x2019;ve always loved, they&#x2019;re telling us they&#x2019;re getting ready to go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F04\u002Fyour-cat-is-trying-to-talk-to-you.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003EYour Cat Is Trying to Talk to You\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMy 30th came and went, and with it the (unfair and silly, not to mention one-sided) &#x201C;agreement&#x201D; I&#x2019;d made with Kitty. I don&#x2019;t know if her health truly unraveled in the weeks after that, or if it was that I finally forced myself to look at it squarely. Probably, it was a little of both. One night, she didn&#x2019;t hop up on the bed with us. Later, I tried and failed to recall the last time I&#x2019;d seen her unwind with some Cat TV. The weekend before her death, she hardly touched her food, even the fanciest of Fancy Feast varietals. The following Monday, she tried to walk toward me but collapsed on her side halfway there, and I couldn&#x2019;t deny it any longer. I gently placed her in her carrier and headed with my boyfriend to the emergency vet for the last time.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThere, the on-duty vet suggested we place her once again in a hyperbaric oxygen chamber, this time for several days. It wasn&#x2019;t guaranteed to help, and would bring the charges to at least $3,000. If we took her home, however, she&#x2019;d almost certainly die, painfully, and within hours. (These were the options laid out for us &#x2014; even then, no explicit mention of euthanasia.) Andrew and I asked for time to talk it over, and when the vet left us in the examination room, he (inadvertently, I assume) left the screen up that showed Kitty&#x2019;s medical records, and we saw the alarming frequency at which she&#x2019;d needed chest taps in recent months. We&#x2019;d already asked so much of her; the vast financial and emotional cost suddenly seemed too great to justify. We knew what we had to do, though even still I made a last attempt to hang on. (&#x201C;You can haunt us if you want!&#x201D; I blurted through my tears, stupidly.)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBefore the vet gave her the initial sedative, which preceded the injection to stop her failing heart, Kitty swiveled her head wildly around the exam room, taking in the grim metal surfaces with wide eyes. I hated that her last moments were spent in such a scary and strange environment, but it was too late to plan for a peaceful good-bye. She had been a very good kitty, and we told her so, as we each stroked her fur. Finally, I let her go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fauthor\u002FMelissa%20Dahl\u002F\"\u003EMelissa Sleep\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca Dreams\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca Alone\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca Face-Blind\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca 10 Cities Where People Dont Look Their Age","summary":"You know how some people just seem to defy the hands of time? Is your city on the list?","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fa153d5a2f17c4541149ea71d3ccf1e57cb43c6a5.jpg\" alt=\"Top 10 Cities Where People Don&#x2019;t Look Their Age\" width=\"540\" height=\"271\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EIs your hometown on the list?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E (Photo: Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EYou know how some people just seem to defy the hands of time? If you live in one of America&#x2019;s youngest-looking cities, there&#x2019;s a chance you&#x2019;re one of those people.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe survey considered&#xA0;lifestyle factors that affect skin aging, like sun exposure, stress, pollution, average sleep logged, fitness levels, and the prevalence of smoking and alcohol consumption &#x2014; looking at American cities with populations over 300,000. &#x201C;We analyzed a handful of data points that doctors say matter most if you want to keep people guessing your age for decades to come,&#x201D; says Tom Seery, founder and CEO of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.realself.com\"\u003ERealSelf.com\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, which \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftrends.realself.com\u002F2015\u002F07\u002F08\u002Ftop-10-cities-staying-young\"\u003Econducted the survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"505\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ff984deef79975ed84f69fed2be658e96967fbedd.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Graphic: Courtesy of Real Self)&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETopping the list of young-looking cities is Minneapolis, Minnesota, where the locals are not only fitter than average, but also get plenty of sleep. Seattle came in second, thanks mostly to the overcast skies that keep sun exposure very low, while San Francisco, clocked in at third place thanks to its active residents who also catch an ample amount of shut-eye. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESalt Lake City has the lowest smoking rate in the U.S., along with low amounts of stress and drinking, bringing it to fourth. Sunny cities like Honolulu and San Diego still cracked the top 10 in spite of all those ultraviolet rays; both boast healthy, slower-paced lifestyles that are antidotes to aging. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMeanwhile, sun-drenched locales accompanied by heavy aging factors sunk some cities. At the bottom of the list is Riverside, CA, which has skyrocketing stress levels (perhaps&#xA0;due to one of the highest unemployment rates in the country), while the smoky and boozy late night culture of Las Vegas has it sitting second-to-last.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fwhy-skin-wrinkles-more-in-certain-areas-123583834227.html\"\u003EWhy Skin Wrinkles More In Certain Areas\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EHigher rates of obesity, smoking, drinking, and poor sleep habits all plummeted cities like New Orleans, Detroit, Albuquerque and Oklahoma City to the bottom of the list. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EExperts say that while skincare products can certainly help skin look younger, it&#x2019;s our daily lifestyles that influence the way we look the most. &#x201C;Age management has to do with managing your stress levels and learning to say &#x2018;no&#x2019; when you&#x2019;re overwhelmed, taking care of yourself and making sure you exercise regularly,&#x201D; says Montclair, New Jersey dermatologist, \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.imagedermatology.com\u002F\"\u003EJeanine B. Downie, MD\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. &#x201C;As we get older, we need to sleep more to help our bodies recover,&#x201D; she adds.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you live in a city with high aging factors, Dr. Downie says staying active is one of the best ways to negate the effects. &#x201C;As you get older, regularly exercising more intensely for shorter bursts of time is one of the best ways to stay fit and young as we age in our stressful society,&#x201D; advises Downie. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EKnown as interval training, research has shown that these shorter 15 to 20 minute bursts of higher intensity exercise (in comparison to longer light or moderate workouts) not only oxygenate the body to help relieve stress, but also offer a variety of anti-aging benefits, including burning more fat and moving sugar out of the bloodstream for healthier blood sugar levels. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERead This Next: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fthe-part-of-your-face-you-absolutely-need-to-122973275813.html\"\u003EThe Part of your Face You Absolutely Need to Protect from the Sun&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELet&#x2019;s keep in touch! Max Amount of Weight You Could Realistically Gain in One Day","summary":"We asked Samantha Cassetty, R.D., M.S., nutrition director at Luvo, just how much weight you can realistically gain in one terrible, horrible, no good, very bad (eating) day.","body":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"The Max Amount of Weight You Could Realistically Gain in One Day\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002Fe9bccb1f29bcb5732d776aab8b3d647cf00a7499.jpg\" width=\"500\" height=\"333\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EEveryone fears the consequence of a diet that has gone off the rails.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E(Food Collection\u002FOffset)\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003EBy Annie Daly for Women&#x2019;s Health&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOf course you try your very best to stick to a relatively healthy diet and exercise plan. But some days, you&#x2019;re bound to go overboard&#x2014;after all, you&#x2019;re only human. Perhaps it&#x2019;s that time of the month and you just can&#x2019;t stop munching; perhaps you had one too many margs at happy hour and find yourself housing enough tacos at dinner to win an eating contest; or perhaps you&#x2019;re so overtired that you double up on breakfast because your stomach feels like a bottomless pit. Point is, everyone overindulges on occasion. But while it&#x2019;s easy to freak out and think you &#x201C;blew your diet,&#x201D; don&#x2019;t&#x2014;because you didn&#x2019;t.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWe asked Samantha Cassetty, R.D., M.S., nutrition director at Luvo, just how much weight you can realistically gain in one terrible, horrible, no good, very bad (eating) day. And it turns out, you&#x2019;d have to take in a \u003Cem\u003Eridiculous\u003C\u002Fem\u003E amount of food to gain even just a pound in one day.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;It&#x2019;s virtually impossible to gain weight overnight, even if you really blew it on bar food,&#x201D; says Cassetty. &#x201C;The reason comes down to calorie math. Though it&#x2019;s not 100 percent precise, the basic principle stands true: In order to gain weight, you&#x2019;d have to eat 3,500&#xA0;\u003Cem\u003Emore\u003C\u002Fem\u003E calories than you typically eat and burn off to maintain your figure.&#x201D; So let&#x2019;s say you eat 2,000 calories per day on a normal day. You&#x2019;d have to eat 3,500&#xA0;\u003Cem\u003Eadditional \u003C\u002Fem\u003Ecalories, totaling 5,500 calories, to gain a single pound. And that&#x2019;s not even taking any physical activity into account.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWhat does 3,500 calories look like, exactly? &#x201C;To get 3,500 more calories, you could eat your regular diet and then also have three glasses of wine (370 calories), two chicken wings (110 calories), some onion rings (340 calories), a portion of chips and queso (290 calories), one burger with the works (860 calories), and a slice of chocolate cake (795 calories). That&#x2019;s a lot of food&#x2014;and you haven&#x2019;t even hit the mark yet!&#x201D; says Cassetty.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere&#x2019;s even more scientific evidence that it&#x2019;s pretty hard to gain real weight after one day of overeating: &#x201C;Although people typically say they gain five to 10 pounds over the six-week holiday period, the best study to date, published in the \u003Cem\u003ENew England Journal of Medicine\u003C\u002Fem\u003E, found that, on average, most people gained just one,&#x201D; says Cassetty. &#x201C;Fewer than 10 percent of the study participants actually gained more than five pounds between Thanksgiving and New Year&#x2019;s Day.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOf course, a bad diet day could leave you feeling incredibly bloated and just &#x201C;ugh&#x201D; the next day. &#x201C;But as long as you course correct the next day&#x2014;i.e., you \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.womenshealthmag.com\u002Fweight-loss\u002Fwhat-to-do-after-eating-too-much?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_StopOvereating\"\u003Eeat responsibly\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;and get back to your\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.womenshealthmag.com\u002Ffitness?cid=Synd_YahooHealth_RealisticWeightGainInDay_Content-WeightLoss_October14_FitnessChannel\"\u003E fitness routine\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#x2014;you&#x2019;ll keep the real pounds from piling on,&#x201D; says Cassetty. So as you go into the holiday season, remember: It&#x2019;s okay if you love your mom&#x2019;s cooking so much that you eat a lot of it. Just don&#x2019;t make a habit of it, and be sure to stay consistent with your gym routine.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAnd if you \u003Cem\u003Edo\u003C\u002Fem\u003E get off track in a more significant way, \u003Ca out what \u003Cem\u003Enot\u003C\u002Fem\u003E to do after you&#x2019;ve gained weight\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E
